function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.256!');

// Dir added: plugins/database/pgsql
@mkdir('plugins/database/pgsql');
if (!is_dir('plugins/database/pgsql')) {
	warn('Directory could not be created: plugins/database/pgsql');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/pgsql', 0755)) {
	warn('Could not change directory permissions of plugins/database/pgsql');
}

// File added: plugins/database/pgsql/index.html
function writefile_1() {
	@$fp = fopen('plugins/database/pgsql/index.html', 'w');
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode(''));
	@fclose($fp);
}
if (is_file('plugins/database/pgsql/index.html') && (sha1_file('plugins/database/pgsql/index.html') != 'da39a3ee5e6b4b0d3255bfef95601890afd80709')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/pgsql/index.html');
	$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/pgsql/index.html');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/database/pgsql/index.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('plugins/database/pgsql/index.html', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('plugins/database/pgsql/index.html')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/pgsql/index.html');
} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/pgsql/index.html') != 'da39a3ee5e6b4b0d3255bfef95601890afd80709') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/pgsql/index.html');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/pgsql/index.html', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/pgsql/index.html');
}

if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'ad39b1c35fe7b1f13eeabbe6bb1cbaedc503121f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'ad39b1c35fe7b1f13eeabbe6bb1cbaedc503121f') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'ec26e007b0f1290828d7c41e89fec63f07b36749') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'ad39b1c35fe7b1f13eeabbe6bb1cbaedc503121f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index.php');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index.php') != '294711663f1d033d6ace729a0fecb577e5468d90') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '294711663f1d033d6ace729a0fecb577e5468d90') {
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '5771e5e284381c78c88f75c0f604228eebe3384c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '294711663f1d033d6ace729a0fecb577e5468d90') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index.php');
		}
	}
}

	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') != '75e7317ab5da5f43a579e174d0446db2c528fee9') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') !== '75e7317ab5da5f43a579e174d0446db2c528fee9') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') !== 'edb3adfb6787bf15dfa8a464d33e76d71808be6e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') !== '75e7317ab5da5f43a579e174d0446db2c528fee9') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php') != '2b060bedcc240656ab5e84c22a08d429eb21ef2a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php') !== '2b060bedcc240656ab5e84c22a08d429eb21ef2a') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php') !== '631f30329e8829930a89e792983f692b2ddd6164') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_13();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php') !== '2b060bedcc240656ab5e84c22a08d429eb21ef2a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');

	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/raPages/102_change_email/plugin.inc.php') != '884d80584f69eddc6e907e0721e92b161cd31b41') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/raPages/102_change_email/plugin.inc.php');

	}

	if (@sha1_file('plugins/raPages/102_change_email/plugin.inc.php') !== '884d80584f69eddc6e907e0721e92b161cd31b41') {

				warn('Creation of backup failed');

if (!is_file('setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
	writefile_21();
	if (!is_file('setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio') != 'd50b45b8f086ab73cbe789c40ec6e2ad85604b38') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio') !== 'd50b45b8f086ab73cbe789c40ec6e2ad85604b38') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio') !== '34424f058b2622135c0f9b55c0dda420d54d1b90') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_21();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio') !== 'd50b45b8f086ab73cbe789c40ec6e2ad85604b38') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
	writefile_22();
	if (!is_file('setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png') != '7999f70b24fe6859fbc6fe83babb2b399e6f801d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png') !== '7999f70b24fe6859fbc6fe83babb2b399e6f801d') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png') !== '7027b1cde97a0557df13f6c5919ca76cd250ae22') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_22();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png') !== '7999f70b24fe6859fbc6fe83babb2b399e6f801d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 257\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 257') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
